<analysis>**original_problem_statement:**
The user initially requested the removal of all iCal (iCalendar) related input fields and UI elements from the Add Property and Edit Property forms, as this functionality was no longer needed. Concurrently, they pointed out that Google Maps links generated by the AI chatbot were not clickable.

During the fixing process, two more issues were identified:
1.  The AI was formatting some words in its responses with markdown bold (e.g., ).
2.  Even when made clickable, the Google Maps links were being blocked by the browser () due to Google's security policies.

After these issues were resolved, the user introduced a major new feature request: to build a custom, offline-first proximity search engine. This system should use a predefined list of points of interest (POIs) for Sarajevo and calculate the nearest locations to a guest's apartment using the Haversine formula, completely removing the dependency on external map APIs for this functionality.

**User's preferred language**: The user's primary language is English, with occasional use of Bosnian/Croatian/Serbian colloquialisms. The next agent should respond in English.

**what currently exists?**
The application consists of a React frontend () and a FastAPI backend (). The agent has successfully completed the following in this session:
-   Removed all iCal-related fields, state, and UI elements from the frontend.
-   Implemented a helper function in React to make URLs in chat messages clickable.
-   Fixed an issue where the AI used unwanted markdown bold formatting by updating the backend prompt and adding a frontend string replacement.
-   Addressed the  issue by implementing a Copy Link button alongside the direct link for all Google Maps URLs, providing a reliable workaround for users.
The application is in a stable state with these fixes applied.
